338#if SIZEOF_INT4 < SIZEOF_LONG8
339static inline int
340rb_long2int_inline(long n)
341{
342 int i = (int)n;
343 if ((long)i != n)
344 rb_out_of_int(n);
345
346 return i;
347}

641# define RUBY_SAFE_LEVEL_INVALID_P(level) \

643 __builtin_choose_expr(\
644 __builtin_constant_p(level), \
645 ((level) < 0 || RUBY_SAFE_LEVEL_MAX1 < (level)), 0))
646# define RUBY_SAFE_LEVEL_CHECK(level, type) \
647 __extension__(__builtin_choose_expr(RUBY_SAFE_LEVEL_INVALID_P(level), ruby_safe_level_2_##type(), (level)))
648# else
649/* in gcc 4.8 or earlier, __builtin_choose_expr() does not consider
650 * __builtin_constant_p(variable) a constant expression.
651 */
652# define RUBY_SAFE_LEVEL_INVALID_P(level) \
653 __extension__(__builtin_constant_p(level) && \
654 ((level) < 0 || RUBY_SAFE_LEVEL_MAX1 < (level)))
655# define RUBY_SAFE_LEVEL_CHECK(level, type) \
656 (RUBY_SAFE_LEVEL_INVALID_P(level) ? ruby_safe_level_2_##type() : (level))
657# endif

670static inline long
671rb_num2long_inline(VALUE x)
672{
673 if (RB_FIXNUM_P(x)(((int)(long)(x))&RUBY_FIXNUM_FLAG))
674 return RB_FIX2LONG(x)((long)(((long)(x))>>(int)(1)));
675 else
676 return rb_num2long(x);
677}
678#define RB_NUM2LONG(x)rb_num2long_inline(x) rb_num2long_inline(x)
679#define NUM2LONG(x)rb_num2long_inline(x) RB_NUM2LONG(x)rb_num2long_inline(x)
680static inline unsigned long
681rb_num2ulong_inline(VALUE x)
682{
683 if (RB_FIXNUM_P(x)(((int)(long)(x))&RUBY_FIXNUM_FLAG))
684 return RB_FIX2ULONG(x)((unsigned long)((long)(((long)(x))>>(int)(1))));
685 else
686 return rb_num2ulong(x);
687}
688#define RB_NUM2ULONG(x)rb_num2ulong_inline(x) rb_num2ulong_inline(x)
689#define NUM2ULONG(x)rb_num2ulong_inline(x) RB_NUM2ULONG(x)rb_num2ulong_inline(x)

720short rb_num2short(VALUE);
721unsigned short rb_num2ushort(VALUE);
722short rb_fix2short(VALUE);
723unsigned short rb_fix2ushort(VALUE);
724#define RB_FIX2SHORT(x)(rb_fix2short((VALUE)(x))) (rb_fix2short((VALUE)(x)))
725#define FIX2SHORT(x)(rb_fix2short((VALUE)(x))) RB_FIX2SHORT(x)(rb_fix2short((VALUE)(x)))
726static inline short
727rb_num2short_inline(VALUE x)
728{
729 if (RB_FIXNUM_P(x)(((int)(long)(x))&RUBY_FIXNUM_FLAG))
730 return rb_fix2short(x);
731 else
732 return rb_num2short(x);
733}

1148struct rb_data_type_struct {
1149 const char *wrap_struct_name;
1150 struct {
1151 void (*dmark)(void*);
1152 void (*dfree)(void*);
1153 size_t (*dsize)(const void *);
1154 void (*dcompact)(void*);

1156 This array *must* be filled with ZERO. */
1157 } function;

1159 void *data; /* This area can be used for any purpose
1160 by a programmer who define the type. */
1161 VALUE flags; /* RUBY_FL_WB_PROTECTED */
1162};

1496
1497/* Write barrier (WB) interfaces:
1498 * - RB_OBJ_WRITE(a, slot, b): WB for new reference from `a' to `b'.
1499 * Write `b' into `*slot'. `slot' is a pointer in `a'.
1500 * - RB_OBJ_WRITTEN(a, oldv, b): WB for new reference from `a' to `b'.
1501 * This doesn't write any values, but only a WB declaration.
1502 * `oldv' is replaced value with `b' (not used in current Ruby).
1503 *
1504 * NOTE: The following core interfaces can be changed in the future.
1505 * Please catch up if you want to insert WB into C-extensions
1506 * correctly.
1507 */
1508#define RB_OBJ_WRITE(a, slot, b)rb_obj_write((VALUE)(a), (VALUE *)(slot), (VALUE)(b), "../.././include/ruby/ruby.h"
, 1508) rb_obj_write((VALUE)(a), (VALUE *)(slot), (VALUE)(b), __FILE__"../.././include/ruby/ruby.h", __LINE__1508)
1509#define RB_OBJ_WRITTEN(a, oldv, b)rb_obj_written((VALUE)(a), (VALUE)(oldv), (VALUE)(b), "../.././include/ruby/ruby.h"
, 1509) rb_obj_written((VALUE)(a), (VALUE)(oldv), (VALUE)(b), __FILE__"../.././include/ruby/ruby.h", __LINE__1509)
1510
1511#ifndef USE_RGENGC_LOGGING_WB_UNPROTECT0
1512#define USE_RGENGC_LOGGING_WB_UNPROTECT0 0
1513#endif
1514
1515#if USE_RGENGC_LOGGING_WB_UNPROTECT0
1516void rb_gc_unprotect_logging(void *objptr, const char *filename, int line);
1517#define RGENGC_LOGGING_WB_UNPROTECT rb_gc_unprotect_logging
1518#endif
1519
1520static inline VALUE
1521rb_obj_wb_unprotect(VALUE x, RB_UNUSED_VAR(const char *filename)const char *filename __attribute__ ((unused)), RB_UNUSED_VAR(int line)int line __attribute__ ((unused)))
1522{
1523#ifdef RGENGC_LOGGING_WB_UNPROTECT
1524 RGENGC_LOGGING_WB_UNPROTECT((void *)x, filename, line);
1525#endif
1526#if USE_RGENGC1
1527 rb_gc_writebarrier_unprotect(x);
1528#endif
1529 return x;
1530}

1532static inline VALUE
1533rb_obj_written(VALUE a, RB_UNUSED_VAR(VALUE oldv)VALUE oldv __attribute__ ((unused)), VALUE b, RB_UNUSED_VAR(const char *filename)const char *filename __attribute__ ((unused)), RB_UNUSED_VAR(int line)int line __attribute__ ((unused)))
1534{
1535#ifdef RGENGC_LOGGING_OBJ_WRITTEN
1536 RGENGC_LOGGING_OBJ_WRITTEN(a, oldv, b, filename, line);
1537#endif
1538
1539#if USE_RGENGC1
1540 if (!RB_SPECIAL_CONST_P(b)(((VALUE)(b) & RUBY_IMMEDIATE_MASK) || !!(((VALUE)(b) &
(VALUE)~((VALUE)RUBY_Qnil)) == 0))) {
1541 rb_gc_writebarrier(a, b);
1542 }
1543#endif

1548static inline VALUE
1549rb_obj_write(VALUE a, VALUE *slot, VALUE b, RB_UNUSED_VAR(const char *filename)const char *filename __attribute__ ((unused)), RB_UNUSED_VAR(int line)int line __attribute__ ((unused)))
1550{
1551#ifdef RGENGC_LOGGING_WRITE

1559#endif
1560 return a;
1561}

1691#if HAVE_LONG_LONG1 && SIZEOF_SIZE_T8 * 2 <= SIZEOF_LONG_LONG8

1696static inline int
1697rb_mul_size_overflow(size_t a, size_t b, size_t max, size_t *c)
1698{
1699#ifdef DSIZE_Tunsigned __int128
1700# ifdef __GNUC__4
1701 __extension__
1702# endif
1703 DSIZE_Tunsigned __int128 c2 = (DSIZE_Tunsigned __int128)a * (DSIZE_Tunsigned __int128)b;
1704 if (c2 > max) return 1;
1705 *c = (size_t)c2;
1706#else
1707 if (b != 0 && a > max / b) return 1;
1708 *c = a * b;
1709#endif
1710 return 0;
1711}
1712static inline void *
1713rb_alloc_tmp_buffer2(volatile VALUE *store, long count, size_t elsize)
1714{
1715 size_t cnt = (size_t)count;
1716 if (elsize == sizeof(VALUE)) {
1717 if (RB_UNLIKELY(cnt > LONG_MAX / sizeof(VALUE))(__builtin_expect(!!(cnt > 9223372036854775807L / sizeof(VALUE
)), 0))) {
1718 ruby_malloc_size_overflow(cnt, elsize);
1719 }
1720 }
1721 else {
1722 size_t size, max = LONG_MAX9223372036854775807L - sizeof(VALUE) + 1;
1723 if (RB_UNLIKELY(rb_mul_size_overflow(cnt, elsize, max, &size))(__builtin_expect(!!(rb_mul_size_overflow(cnt, elsize, max, &
size)), 0))) {
1724 ruby_malloc_size_overflow(cnt, elsize);
1725 }
1726 cnt = (size + sizeof(VALUE) - 1) / sizeof(VALUE);
1727 }
1728 return rb_alloc_tmp_buffer_with_count(store, cnt * sizeof(VALUE), cnt);
1729}

2092static inline VALUE
2093rb_class_of(VALUE obj)
2094{
2095 if (RB_IMMEDIATE_P(obj)((VALUE)(obj) & RUBY_IMMEDIATE_MASK)) {
2096 if (RB_FIXNUM_P(obj)(((int)(long)(obj))&RUBY_FIXNUM_FLAG)) return rb_cInteger;
2097 if (RB_FLONUM_P(obj)((((int)(long)(obj))&RUBY_FLONUM_MASK) == RUBY_FLONUM_FLAG
)) return rb_cFloat;
2098 if (obj == RUBY_Qtrue((VALUE)RUBY_Qtrue)) return rb_cTrueClass;
2099 if (RB_STATIC_SYM_P(obj)(((VALUE)(obj)&~((~(VALUE)0)<<RUBY_SPECIAL_SHIFT)) ==
RUBY_SYMBOL_FLAG)) return rb_cSymbol;
2100 }
2101 else if (!RB_TEST(obj)!(((VALUE)(obj) & (VALUE)~((VALUE)RUBY_Qnil)) == 0)) {
2102 if (obj == RUBY_Qnil((VALUE)RUBY_Qnil)) return rb_cNilClass;
2103 if (obj == RUBY_Qfalse((VALUE)RUBY_Qfalse)) return rb_cFalseClass;
2104 }
2105 return RBASIC(obj)((struct RBasic*)(obj))->klass;
2106}

2108static inline int
2109rb_type(VALUE obj)
2110{
2111 if (RB_IMMEDIATE_P(obj)((VALUE)(obj) & RUBY_IMMEDIATE_MASK)) {
2112 if (RB_FIXNUM_P(obj)(((int)(long)(obj))&RUBY_FIXNUM_FLAG)) return RUBY_T_FIXNUM;
2113 if (RB_FLONUM_P(obj)((((int)(long)(obj))&RUBY_FLONUM_MASK) == RUBY_FLONUM_FLAG
)) return RUBY_T_FLOAT;
2114 if (obj == RUBY_Qtrue((VALUE)RUBY_Qtrue)) return RUBY_T_TRUE;
2115 if (RB_STATIC_SYM_P(obj)(((VALUE)(obj)&~((~(VALUE)0)<<RUBY_SPECIAL_SHIFT)) ==
RUBY_SYMBOL_FLAG)) return RUBY_T_SYMBOL;
2116 if (obj == RUBY_Qundef((VALUE)RUBY_Qundef)) return RUBY_T_UNDEF;
2117 }
2118 else if (!RB_TEST(obj)!(((VALUE)(obj) & (VALUE)~((VALUE)RUBY_Qnil)) == 0)) {
2119 if (obj == RUBY_Qnil((VALUE)RUBY_Qnil)) return RUBY_T_NIL;
2120 if (obj == RUBY_Qfalse((VALUE)RUBY_Qfalse)) return RUBY_T_FALSE;
2121 }
2122 return RB_BUILTIN_TYPE(obj)(int)(((struct RBasic*)(obj))->flags & RUBY_T_MASK);
2123}

2287static inline int rb_isascii(int c){ return '\0' <= c && c <= '\x7f'; }
2288static inline int rb_isupper(int c){ return 'A' <= c && c <= 'Z'; }
2289static inline int rb_islower(int c){ return 'a' <= c && c <= 'z'; }
2290static inline int rb_isalpha(int c){ return rb_isupper(c) || rb_islower(c); }
2291static inline int rb_isdigit(int c){ return '0' <= c && c <= '9'; }
2292static inline int rb_isalnum(int c){ return rb_isalpha(c) || rb_isdigit(c); }
2293static inline int rb_isxdigit(int c){ return rb_isdigit(c) || ('A' <= c && c <= 'F') || ('a' <= c && c <= 'f'); }
2294static inline int rb_isblank(int c){ return c == ' ' || c == '\t'; }
2295static inline int rb_isspace(int c){ return c == ' ' || ('\t' <= c && c <= '\r'); }
2296static inline int rb_iscntrl(int c){ return ('\0' <= c && c < ' ') || c == '\x7f'; }
2297static inline int rb_isprint(int c){ return ' ' <= c && c <= '\x7e'; }
2298static inline int rb_ispunct(int c){ return !rb_isalnum(c); }
2299static inline int rb_isgraph(int c){ return '!' <= c && c <= '\x7e'; }
2300static inline int rb_tolower(int c) { return rb_isupper(c) ? (c|0x20) : c; }
2301static inline int rb_toupper(int c) { return rb_islower(c) ? (c&0x5f) : c; }
